%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/dependent-types/ImplicationDirectIntroductionDTL.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/dependent-types/ImplicationDirectIntroductionDTL.metta')
;;; MeTTa port of the Implication Direct Introduction PLN rule, encoded
;;; as dependent types, i.e. propositions as types.
;;;
;;; See ImplicationDirectIntroductionEntail.metta for more detail on a
;;; pseudo formal description.
;;;
;;; In the case of dependent types, inference rules are constructors of
;;; the propositions to be proven.  Then a proof is an tree composed of
;;; calls of such constructors.
;;;
;;; For instance assuming two inference rules
;;;
;;; ImplicationDirectIntroduction (IDI, for short)
;;; Deduction (DED, for short)
;;;
;;; The following inference tree
;;;
;;; ...            ...
;;; -----(IDI)     -----(IDI)
;;; P → Q          Q → R
;;; ---------------------(DED)
;;;         P → R
;;;
;;; is represented by the following MeTTa expression
;;;
;;; (Deduction
;;;    (ImplicationDirectIntroduction ...)
;;;    (ImplicationDirectIntroduction ...))
;;;
;;; where the premises of ImplicationDirectIntroduction are left
;;; undefined for now.
;;;
;;; How such propositions as types can be defined still remains to be
;;; determined but ideally it may look something like
;;;
;;; (: Deduction
;;;    (-> (≞ (→ $P $Q) $TV1)
;;;        (≞ (→ $Q $R) $TV2)
;;;        (≞ (→ $P $R) (deduction-formula $TV1 $TV2))))
;;;
;;; where ≞, → are dependent types, and formula is just a regular metta
;;; function.
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta")

; !(import! &self "../common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta")
% DEBUG: eval_args(100,'&self',['import!','&self','../common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta'],OUT).

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta')
;;; Evidential truth value type. Represent a truth value alongside its
;;; evidence.

% DEBUG: eval_args(100,'&self',['import!','&self','TruthValue.metta'],OUT).

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Pr',[->,'Number','TruthValue']])
  (: Pr 
    (-> Number TruthValue))


;;; Simple Truth Value.  A Second order probability TV constructor,
;;; i.e. probability and confidence.  The probability is in fact the
;;; mode of the corresponding beta distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: STV 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Constants ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; For now the underlying beta distributions have a Jeffreys prior,
;;; i.e. the prior alpha and beta are 0.5.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-alpha',[->,'Number']])
  (: prior-alpha 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['prior-alpha'],0.5])
  (= 
    (prior-alpha) 0.5)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-beta',[->,'Number']])
  (: prior-beta 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['prior-beta'],0.5])
  (= 
    (prior-beta) 0.5)


;;; Lookahead
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,lookahead,[->,'Number']])
  (: lookahead 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[lookahead],1.0])
  (= 
    (lookahead) 1.0)


;;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'max-count',[->,'Number']])
  (: max-count 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['max-count'],1000000000.0])
  (= 
    (max-count) 1000000000.0)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;;
;;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;;; Increment the negative count of a given truth value, by
;;; incrementing its total count without incrementing the positive
;;; count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: inc-neg-count 
    (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['inc-neg-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,Pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]]])
  (= 
    (inc-neg-count 
      (STV $S $C)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Tot_cnt 
          (confidence->count $C)) 
        ($Pos_cnt 
          (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
        ($New_tot_cnt 
          (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
      (STV 
        (/ $Pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
        (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;;; Increment the positive count of a given truth value, by
;;; incrementing its total count and its positive count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: inc-pos-count 
    (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['inc-pos-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_pos_cnt,[+,Pos_cnt,1]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,New_pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]]])
  (= 
    (inc-pos-count 
      (STV $S $C)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Tot_cnt 
          (confidence->count $C)) 
        ($Pos_cnt 
          (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
        ($New_pos_cnt 
          (+ $Pos_cnt 1)) 
        ($New_tot_cnt 
          (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
      (STV 
        (/ $New_pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
        (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mode 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0])
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0])
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr])
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr])
  (= 
    (mode 
      (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;;; be supported at the moment).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count']])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Bl $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count']])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Pr $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf]])
  (= 
    (count 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) 
    (confidence->count $Conf))


;;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;;; notion of confidence, such as STV, the formula to convert a count
;;; into confidence is as follows
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: confidence 
    (-> TruthValue Number))

      (prior-beta)

;;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/formula/ImplicationDirectIntroductionFormula.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/formula/ImplicationDirectIntroductionFormula.metta')
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Rule Definition ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; All rules are implemented as constructors of propositions encoded
;;; as types.
;;; To deal with an abritrary number of pieces of evidence the rule is
;;; defined inductively.
;;; Base case (one piece of evidence):
;;;
;;; (p a) = True
;;; (q a) = qa
;;; â¢
;;; pâq â (ETV (:: a â) tv)
;;;
;;; where tv is calculated according to the direct introduction
;;; formula.  Note that we don't bother to take into account pieces of
;;; evidence that is not True on (p a), because it has no impact on the
;;; resulting truth value otherwise.
;;;
;;; To avoid prematurely reducing (p a) = pa to pa = pa, the following
;;; representation is used instead
;;;
;;; (â· p a pa)
;;;
;;; which can be read as "under p, the image of a is pa".
;;;
;;; â· is essentially the Atomese equivalent of ExecutionLink.  It has
;;; description: IMAGE OF, hexadecimal code: 0x22B7, unicode-math code:
;;; \imageof and latex code: \multimapdotbothB.
;;; Formula for the inductive Implication Direct Introduction rule.
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta")

; !(import! &self "../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta")
% DEBUG: eval_args(100,'&self',['import!','&self','../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta'],OUT).

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/TruthValue.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/TruthValue.metta')

%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_88/hyperon-pln_metta/common/Num.metta')

  (: max

;;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;;
;;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))

;;; Recursive step (more than one piece of evidence):
;;;
;;; (p a) = True
;;; (q a) = qa
;;; pâq â (ETV (:: h t) pqtv)
;;; h < a
;;; â¢
;;; pâq â (ETV (:: a (:: h t)) tv)
;;;
;;; where tv is calculated using the direct introduction formula.  Note
;;; that we don't bother to take into account pieces of evidence that
;;; is not True on (p a), because it has no impact on the resulting
;;; truth value otherwise.
;;;
;;; To avoid prematurely reducing (p a) = pa to pa = pa, the following
;;; representation is used instead
;;;
;;; (â· p a pa)
;;;
;;; which can be read as "under p, the image of a is pa".
;;;
;;; For a similar reason, the premise h < a is represented as
;;;
;;; h â a
;;;
;;; â is the axiomatized version of <.  It is defined in Num.metta.
;;; The box around the less than sign is here to manifest its
;;; axiomatic, as opposed to computational, nature.  It has
;;; description: APL FUNCTIONAL SYMBOL QUAD LESS-THAN and hexadecimal
;;; code: 0x2343.
;;;
;;; The h â a premise is there to garanty that evidence is not double
;;; counted.
;;;
;;; Historical note: initially the premise
;;;
;;; h â a
;;;
;;; was replaced by
;;;
;;; a â (:: h t)
;;;
;;; But then it was realized that it is far more efficient to enforce
;;; the order in which evidence can be pilled up, than to prove that a
;;; new piece of evidence does not belongs to an existing evidence set.
;;; And now you know why time is the way it is.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'implication-direct-introduction-recursive-rule',[->,'Atom']])
  (: implication-direct-introduction-recursive-rule 
    (-> Atom))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['implication-direct-introduction-recursive-rule'],[:,'IDIRecursive',[->,['â\x8A\·',P,A,'True'],['â\x8A\·',Q,A,Qa],['â\x89\\x9E\',['â\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',[::,H,T],Pqtv]],['â\x8D\\x83\',H,A],['â\x89\\x9E\',['â\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',[::,A,[::,H,T]],['direct-introduction-recursive-formula',Qa,Pqtv]]]]]])
  (= 
    (implication-direct-introduction-recursive-rule) 
    (: IDIRecursive 
      (-> 
        (â· $P $A True) 
        (â· $Q $A $Qa) 
        (â 
          (â $P $Q) 
          (ETV 
            (:: $H $T) $Pqtv)) 
        (â $H $A) 
        (â 
          (â $P $Q) 
          (ETV 
            (:: $A 
              (:: $H $T)) 
            (direct-introduction-recursive-formula $Qa $Pqtv))))))

  (=

;;; !(import! &self Unify.metta)
;;; Enumerate all programs up to a given depth that are consistent with
;;; the query, using the given axiom non-deterministic functions and rules.
;;;
;;; The arguments are:
;;;
;;; $query: an Atom under the form (: TERM TYPE).  The atom may contain
;;;         free variables within TERM and TYPE to form various sort of
;;;         queries, such as:
;;;         1. Backward chaining: (: $term (Inheritance $x Mammal))
;;;         2. Forward chaining: (: ($rule $premise AXIOM) $type)
;;;         3. Mixed chaining: (: ($rule $premise AXIOM) (Inheritance $x Mammal))
;;;         4. Type checking: (: TERM TYPE)
;;;         5. Type inference: (: TERM $type)
;;;
;;; $kb: a nullary function to axiom, to non-deterministically pick up
;;;      an axiom.  An axiom is an Atom of the form (: TERM TYPE).
;;;
;;; $rb: a nullary function to rule, to non-deterministically pick up a
;;;      rule.  A rule is a function mapping premises to conclusion,
;;;      where premises and conclusion have the form (: TERM TYPE).
;;;
;;; $depth: a Nat representing the maximum depth of the generated
;;;         programs.
;;;
;;; TODO: recurse over curried rules instead of duplicating code over
;;; tuples.
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: max 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y]])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;;; Define min
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: min 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y]])
  (= 
    (min $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
  (: clamp 
    (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]]])
  (= 
    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))


;;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
  (: abs 
    (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X]])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (if 
      (< $X 0) 
      (* -1 $X) $X))


;;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: <= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]]])
  (= 
    (<= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (< $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: >= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]]])
  (= 
    (>= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (> $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;;; Define approximately equal
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,approxEq,[->,A,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: approxEq 
    (-> $A $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon]])
  (= 
    (approxEq $X $Y $Epsilon) 
    (<= 
      (abs 
        (- $X $Y)) $Epsilon))


;;; Define Nat
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Nat','Type'])
  (: Nat Type)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Z','Nat'])
  (: Z Nat)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'S',[->,'Nat','Nat']])
  (: S 
    (-> Nat Nat))


;;; Define cast functions between Nat and Number
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNumber,[->,'Number','Nat']])
  (: fromNumber 
    (-> Number Nat))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[fromNumber,N],[if,[<=,N,0],'Z',['S',[fromNumber,[-,N,1]]]]])
  (= 
    (fromNumber $N) 
    (if 
      (<= $N 0) Z 
      (S 
        (fromNumber 
          (- $N 1)))))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNat,[->,'Nat','Number']])
  (: fromNat 
    (-> Nat Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[fromNat,'Z'],0])
  (= 
    (fromNat Z) 0)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[fromNat,['S',K]],[+,1,[fromNat,K]]])
  (= 
    (fromNat 
      (S $K)) 
    (+ 1 
      (fromNat $K)))


;;; Define a generic less than operator, â©», for Nat.  < cannot be used
;;; because it is a built-in, its type is hardwired and cannot be
;;; overloaded.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'â©»',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])
  (: â©» 
    (-> Nat Nat Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»',_,'Z'],'False'])
  (= 
    (â©» $_ Z) False)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»','Z',['S',_]],'True'])
  (= 
    (â©» Z 
      (S $_)) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»',['S',X],['S',Y]],['â©»',X,Y]])
  (= 
    (â©» 
      (S $X) 
      (S $Y)) 
    (â©» $X $Y))


;;; Overload â©» for Number.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'â©»',[->,'Number','Number','Bool']])
  (: â©» 
    (-> Number Number Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»',X,Y],[<,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (â©» $X $Y) 
    (< $X $Y))


;;; Return the ceiling of a non negative number.  If the number is
;;; negative it returns 1.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,ceil,[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: ceil 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[ceil,N],[fromNat,[fromNumber,N]]])
  (= 
    (ceil $N) 
    (fromNat 
      (fromNumber $N)))


;;; Convert Number to Bool.  Anything above 0 converts to True.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'number->bool',[->,'Number','Bool']])
  (: number->bool 
    (-> Number Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['number->bool',X],[<,0,X]])
  (= 
    (number->bool $X) 
    (< 0 $X))


;;; Convert Bool to Number.  False converts to 0, True converts to 1.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'bool->number',[->,'Bool','Number']])
  (: bool->number 
    (-> Bool Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['bool->number','False'],0])
  (= 
    (bool->number False) 0)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['bool->number','True'],1])
  (= 
    (bool->number True) 1)

;;; than â©» as it is a type, not an operator.  Inhabitants of (â x y)
;;; are proofs that x â©» y == True.  For now â is only axiomatized for
;;; Nat.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'â\x8D\\x83\',[->,T,T,'Type']])

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,['zero-lt-succ-axiom'],[->,'Atom']])

;;; If x â y then (S x) â (S y)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,['succ-monotonicity-rule'],[->,'Atom']])
  (:

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,synthesize,[->,'Atom',[->,'Atom'],[->,'Atom'],'Nat','Atom']])
  (: synthesize

;;; Nullary rule (axiom)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,Depth],[let,Query,[Kb],Query]])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb $Depth) 
    (let $Query 
      ($Kb) $Query))


;;; Unary rule
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,[synthesize,Query,Kb,Rb,['S',K]],['let*',[[[:,Ructor,[->,Premise,Conclusion]],[Rb]],[[:,[Ructor,Proof],Conclusion],Query],[[:,Proof,Premise],[synthesize,[:,Proof,Premise],Kb,Rb,K]]],Query]])
  (= 
    (synthesize $Query $Kb $Rb 
      (S $K)) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (: $Ructor 
            (-> $Premise $Conclusion)) 
          ($Rb)) 
        ( (: 
            ($Ructor $Proof) $Conclusion) $Query) 
        ( (: $Proof $Premise) 
          (synthesize 
            (: $Proof $Premise) $Kb $Rb $K))) $Query))

  (=

      (S $K))

            (-> $Premise1 $Premise2 $Conclusion))
